# <a name="hlsl-errors-and-warnings"></a><span data-ttu-id="46be4-103">HLSL 錯誤和警告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="46be4-103">HLSL errors and warnings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="46be4-104">著色器可以傳回的錯誤和警告碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="46be4-104">Error and warning codes that a shader can return.</span></span>
